For a little high culture, head to the Basilica of San Giovanni and the nearby Scala Santa (Holy Steps) which were supposed to have been the steps that Jesus walked on before his trial with Pontius Pilate and were transferred to Rome from Jerusalem in the 4th century. For a place to enjoy a peaceful walk or a quiet sit down, the Appia Antica Park is an ideal haven away from the noise of the city and is filled with archaeological monuments and large trees. The Terme di Caracalla is one of Rome’s most awe-inspiring ruins, with the 1800-year old complex once being Emperor Caracalla’s bathhouse, gym and library. Shopping lovers can find a brilliant selection of outlets on the Via Appia Nuova and browse unique stalls at the lively Via Sannio flea market.
